		SetNumber(caras);

		VehicleFuel[caras] = fuelmeplease;
		VehInfo[caras][pEngine] = 0;
		VehInfo[caras][pLights] = 0;
		VehInfo[caras][pAlarm] = 0;
		VehInfo[caras][pDoors] = 0;
		VehInfo[caras][pBonnet] = 0;
		VehInfo[caras][pBoot] = 0;
		VehInfo[caras][pObjective] = 0;
		VehInfo[caras][pText] = false;
		SetVehicleParamsEx(caras,VehInfo[caras][pEngine],VehInfo[caras][pLights],VehInfo[caras][pAlarm],VehInfo[caras][pDoors],VehInfo[caras][pBonnet],VehInfo[caras][pBoot],VehInfo[caras][pObjective]);
	}
	return 1;
}
public OnGameModeExit()
{
    KillTimer(mtimer);
	SaveStoreGrove();
	SaveStoreBallas();
	SaveStoreAztec();
	SaveStoreVagos();
	SaveStoreRifa();
	SaveGangsStores();
	SaveMafiaStores();
	SaveArmyStores();
	SaveMiner();

	foreach(new i: Player)
	{
		if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
		{
			if(login_check[i] == true)
			{
				SaveAll(i);
				OnPlayerSave(i);
			}
		}
	}
	if(loadfs == true)
	{
		mysql_query(dbHandle,"TRUNCATE TABLE `election`",false);
		Delete3DTextLabel(TextAS[0]);
		Delete3DTextLabel(TextAS[1]);
		Delete3DTextLabel(TextAS[2]);
		Delete3DTextLabel(TextAS[3]);
		Delete3DTextLabel(TextAS[4]);
		Delete3DTextLabel(TextAS[5]);
		DestroyPickup(bulleten);
		DestroyPickup(bull1);
		DestroyPickup(bull2);
		DestroyPickup(bull3);
		foreach(Player, i)
		{
			if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
			{
				RemoveBuildingForPlayer(i, 3861,358.7000100,195.6000100,1014.4000200, 0.25);
				RemoveBuildingForPlayer(i, 2435,340.0000000,191.5000000,1013.2000100, 0.25);
				RemoveBuildingForPlayer(i, 2435,340.0000000,193.6000100,1013.2000100, 0.25);
				RemoveBuildingForPlayer(i, 2435,340.0000000,195.7000000,1013.2000100, 0.25);
				RemoveBuildingForPlayer(i, 1641,340.8496100,193.2656300,1013.0331400, 0.25);
				RemoveBuildingForPlayer(i, 1641,339.5117200,193.7353500,1013.0253300, 0.25);
				RemoveBuildingForPlayer(i, 2290,373.2999900,172.1000100,1013.2000100, 0.25);
				RemoveBuildingForPlayer(i, 2290,373.2999900,177.2000000,1013.2000100, 0.25);
			}
		}
		loadfs = false;
		votego = false;
		votestart = false;
	}
	mysql_close();
	return 1;
}
public OnPlayerConnect(playerid)
{
    PlayerInfo[playerid][pChoosingSkinRegen] = false;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][preg] = false;

	ban_dice[playerid] = 0;
	posadka[playerid] = 0;
	posadka1[playerid] = 0;

	hands_down[playerid] = 0;
	//ban_dice[playerid] = 0;

	}

 	return 1;
}
public OnPlayerDisconnect(playerid, reason)
{
	SetPlayerColor(playerid, COLOR_GRAD);
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pRabota] = 0;
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][gps] == true)
	{
		PlayerInfo[playerid][gps] = false;
		RemovePlayerMapIcon(playerid, 3);
	}
    if(TempAdmin[playerid] == true)
	{
	    PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] = 0;
	    TempAdmin[playerid] = false;
	}
	anti_cheat[playerid][pFlood] = false;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pTimer] = 0;
	GetPlayerMetall[playerid] = 0;
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][cuff] == true)
	{
		new star[80];
		format(star,sizeof(star),"%s[%i] выходит при аресте (+30 минут заключения)", PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],playerid);
		SendClientMessageToAll(COLOR_LIGHTRED,star);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pJailed] = 1;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pJailTime] = 30;
	}
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][preg] == true && PlayerInfo[playerid][pChoosingSkinRegen] == true)
	{
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSex] == 1) PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin] = 230;
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSex] == 2) PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin] = 13;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin] = 239;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pLevel] = 1;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] = 125;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pRadio] = 1;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pCheckTime] = 1;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][0] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][1] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][2] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][3] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][4] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][5] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][6] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][7] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][8] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][9] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][10] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pLeader] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnit] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pPhone] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pPhoneMoney] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pWanted] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pUpdate] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pDrugs] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pAmmo] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMetal] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pJob] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pRang] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pFuel] = 999;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse] = 999;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSila] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMask] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pHeal] = 0;
		//PlayerInfo[playerid][pBusiness] = 999;
		strmid(PlayerInfo[playerid][pWedding], "--", 0, 3, 255);
		SColor(playerid);
		new sasdad [144], temper [32];
		mysql_real_escape_string (PlayerInfo[playerid][pName], temper);
 		format(sasdad, sizeof sasdad, "SELECT * FROM `accounts` WHERE `name` = '%s' LIMIT 1", temper);//Выводим в коллбэк аккаун где логин и пароль равны мени игрока и введённому паролю
 		mysql_pquery(dbHandle, sasdad, "PlayerRegister", "i", playerid);
		anti_cheat[playerid][pTimerAC] = 5;
	}
 	PlayerInfo[playerid][animloading] = false;
	if(AdInfo[pID] == playerid) AdInfo[pAdOpen] = false;
	CASH[playerid] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pDay] = false;
	anti_cheat[playerid][pRequest] = false;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pChoosingSkinRegen] = false;
	if(PlayerStartJob[playerid] == true) PlayerStartJob[playerid] = false;
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pShaxterMetall] > 0)
	{
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pShaxterMetall]*3;
	}
	if(IsValidDynamicObject(gruzobject[playerid]))
    {
        DestroyDynamicObject(gruzobject[playerid]);
    }
 	if(koikame[playerid] < 57)
	{
		koika[koikame[playerid]] = false;
		Updatetext_hospital(koikame[playerid]);
		koikame[playerid] = 57;
		bolkam[playerid] = false;
	}
	strmid(PlayerInfo[playerid][pEmail], "-", 0, 2, 255);
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pShaxter] = false;
	anti_cheat[playerid][pTimerAC] = 0;

	PlayerInfo[playerid][pShaxterMetall] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pTimerShaxter] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pASHG] = 0;
	foreach(new i: Player)
	{
		if(GetPlayerState(i) == PLAYER_STATE_SPECTATING && SpecPlayerID[i] == playerid)
		{
			TogglePlayerSpectating(i, 0);
			gSpectateID[i] = INVALID_PLAYER_ID;
			gSpectateType[i] = ADMIN_SPEC_TYPE_NONE;
			HideMenuForPlayer(spmenu,i);
			sp[i] = true;
			SpawnPlayer(i),anti_cheat[i][pTimerAC] = 10,anti_cheat[i][pOpen] = true;
		}
	}
	CancelSelectTextDraw(playerid);
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pJob] == 1 && PlayerInfo[playerid][BusTarif] > 0)
	{
		SetVehicleToRespawn(PlayerInfo[playerid][CarJobID]);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][BusTarif] = 0;
		Delete3DTextLabel(textjob[playerid]);
		DisablePlayerRaceCheckpoint(playerid);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][Busa] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][RaceBus] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash];
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash] = 0;
	}
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pJob] == 2 && PlayerInfo[playerid][TaxiTarif] > 0)
	{
		SetVehicleToRespawn(PlayerInfo[playerid][CarJobID]);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][TaxiTarif] = 0;
		Delete3DTextLabel(textjob[playerid]);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash];
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash] = 0;
	}
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pJob] == 3 && PlayerInfo[playerid][AirTarif] > 0)
	{
		SetVehicleToRespawn(PlayerInfo[playerid][CarJobID]);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][AirTarif] = 0;
		Delete3DTextLabel(textjob[playerid]);
		DisablePlayerRaceCheckpoint(playerid);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][Ausa] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][RaceAir] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash];
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash] = 0;
	}
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pJob] == 5 && PlayerInfo[playerid][Mehan] == true)
	{
		SetVehicleToRespawn(PlayerInfo[playerid][CarJobID]);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][Mehan] = false;
		Delete3DTextLabel(textjob[playerid]);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] += PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash];
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash] = 0;
	}
	SaveAll(playerid);
	
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pCover] >= 1) PlayerInfo[playerid][pCover] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pArmour] = 0.0;
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] > 0)
	{
	    clear_admin_combo(playerid);
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pLeader] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnit] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pRang] = 0;
	}
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pLoto] = false;
	RemovePlayerAttachedObject(playerid, 1);
	RemovePlayerAttachedObject(playerid, 2);
	RemovePlayerAttachedObject(playerid, 3);
	RemovePlayerAttachedObject(playerid, 4);
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pPatronPlayer] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][CarJobID] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pScore] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pMcore] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdv] = 0;
	DisablePlayerRaceCheckpoint(playerid);
	SaveAll(playerid);
	Clearweapon_anti_cheat(playerid);
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,CaptureBox[playerid]);
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,CaptureTime[playerid]);
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,CaptureWarGang[playerid]);
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,CaptureWarGang2[playerid]);
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,AffectBox[playerid]);
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,AffectTime[playerid]);
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,AffectWarGang[playerid]);
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,AffectWarGang2[playerid]);
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pLeader] = 0;
	DisablePlayerCheckpoint(playerid);
	secondtimer[playerid] = 0;
	OkayInfo[playerid][pChangeOn] = false;
	PlayerTextDrawDestroy(playerid,logo_td[playerid]);
	warpass[playerid] = 0;
	posadka[playerid] = 0;
	posadka1[playerid] = 0;
	posadka2[playerid] = 0;
	sp[playerid] = false;
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse] < 999 && HouseInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse]][hCar] > 0) DestroyVehicle(caridhouse[playerid]);

	PlayerInfo[playerid][pPassword] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][preg] = false;
	login_check[playerid] = false;
	caridhouse[playerid] = 0;
	PlayerInfo[playerid][pCash] = 0;
	if(anti_cheat[playerid][pObject] > 0)
	{
		Delete3DTextLabel(anti_cheat[playerid][pText]);
		DestroyObject(anti_cheat[playerid][pObject]);
		anti_cheat[playerid][pObject] = 0;
	}
	ClearPlayerVars(playerid);
	// =================== [Caligula] =========================================
 	if(GetPVarInt (playerid, "p_sm_used"))
	{
		PlayerTextDrawDestroy (playerid, sm_ptd [playerid]);
		sm_ptd [playerid] = PlayerText:INVALID_TEXT_DRAW;
		for(new i = 0; i < 4; i ++)
		{
			TextDrawHideForPlayer (playerid, sm_td [i]);
		}
		new p_sm = GetPVarInt (playerid, "p_sm_used");
		new i = (p_sm * 2 + (p_sm - 2)) - 1;
		MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i], sm_slot_coord [i] [0], sm_slot_coord [i] [1], sm_slot_coord [i] [2], 1, sm_slot_coord [i] [3], sm_slot_coord [i] [4], sm_slot_coord [i] [5]);
		MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i + 1], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [0], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [1], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [2], 1, sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [3], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [4], sm_slot_coord [i + 1] [5]);
		MoveDynamicObject (sm_slot [i + 2], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [0], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [1], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [2], 1, sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [3], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [4], sm_slot_coord [i + 2] [5]);

		sm_used [p_sm - 1] = false;
	}
	return 1;
}
public OnPlayerSpawn(playerid)
{
	if(PlayerInfo[playerid][preg] == true && PlayerInfo[playerid][pChoosingSkinRegen] == false)
	{
		SetPlayerPos(playerid,1760.7727,-1903.9078,13.565);
		SetPlayerFacingAngle(playerid,271.3320);
		SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_ORANGE, "Вы не прошли регистрацию до конца!");
		SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_ORANGE, "Введите /q чтобы выйти");
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSex] == 1) PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin] = 230;
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSex] == 2) PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkin] = 13;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pLevel] = 1;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pMoney] = 3500;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pRadio] = 1;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pCheckTime] = 1;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][0] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][1] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][2] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][3] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][4] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][5] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][6] = 0;
		PlayerInfo[playerid][pSkill][7] = 0;
